Source Code

These source-code files are part of a reconstructed copy of Luminary 173, the second (unflown) release of the Apollo 14 Lunar Module (LM) Apollo Guidance Computer (AGC) software.

The reconstruction began with reconstructed source code for Luminary 178. Changes between revision 173 and 178 were backed out, as described by Luminary memo 167 (revision 1). The reconstruction was verified by matching memory-bank checksums to those listed in drawing 2021152N. Note that page numbers in the reconstructed code match those for the baseline log section mentioned in each file's changelog; the page numbers for a real Luminary 173 listing would be different.

Comments from the original source code are prefixed with a single '#' symbol, whereas comments added later are prefixed by "##" or "###". Report any errors noted by creating an issue report at the Virtual AGC project's GitHub repository. 

021710,000002:                                                                                                  ## Copyright:   Public domain.
021711,000003:                                                                                                  ## Filename:    P20-P25.agc
021712,000004:                                                                                                  ## Purpose:     A section of Luminary revision 173.
021713,000005:                                                                                                  ##              It is part of the reconstructed source code for the second
021714,000006:                                                                                                  ##              (unflown) release of the flight software for the Lunar
021715,000007:                                                                                                  ##              Module's (LM) Apollo Guidance Computer (AGC) for Apollo 14.
021716,000008:                                                                                                  ##              The code has been recreated from a reconstructed copy of
021717,000009:                                                                                                  ##              Luminary 178, as well as Luminary memo 167 (revision 1).
021718,000010:                                                                                                  ##              It has been adapted such that the resulting bugger words
021719,000011:                                                                                                  ##              exactly match those specified for Luminary 173 in NASA
021720,000012:                                                                                                  ##              drawing 2021152N, which gives relatively high confidence
021721,000013:                                                                                                  ##              that the reconstruction is correct.
021722,000014:                                                                                                  ## Reference:   pp. 500-611
021723,000015:                                                                                                  ## Assembler:   yaYUL
021724,000016:                                                                                                  ## Contact:     Ron Burkey <info@sandroid.org>.
021725,000017:                                                                                                  ## Website:     www.ibiblio.org/apollo/index.html
021726,000018:                                                                                                  ## Mod history: 2019-09-18 MAS  Created from Luminary 178.

021729,000021:                                                                                                  #  RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION PROGRAM 20
021730,000022:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
021731,000023:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 2
021732,000024:                                                                                                  #  BY  P. VOLANTE
021733,000025:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
021734,000026: 
021735,000027:                                                                                                  #    THE PURPOSE OF THIS PROGRAM IS TO CONTROL THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR FROM
021736,000028:                                                                                                  #  STARTUP THROUGH ACQUISITION AND LOCKON TO THE CSM AND TO UPDATE EITHER 
021737,000029:                                                                                                  #  THE LM OR CSM STATE VECTOR (AS SPECIFIED BY THE ASTRONAUT BY DSKY ENTRY)
021738,000030:                                                                                                  #  ON THE BASIS OF THE RR TRACKING DATA.
021739,000031:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
021740,000032: 
021741,000033:                                                                                                  #  ASTRONAUT REQUEST THROUGH DSKY V37E20E
021742,000034:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
021743,000035:                                                                                                  #    R02BOTH (IMU STATUS CHECK)               FLAGUP
021744,000036:                                                                                                  #    GOFLASH (PINBALL-DISPLAY)                FLAGDOWN
021745,000037:                                                                                                  #    R23LEM  (MANUAL ACQUISITION)             BANKCALL
021746,000038:                                                                                                  #    LS201   (LOS DETERMINATION)              TASKOVER
021747,000039:                                                                                                  #    LS202   (RANGE LIMIT TEST)
021748,000040:                                                                                                  #    R61LEM  (PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE)
021749,000041:                                                                                                  #    R21LEM  (RR DESIGNATE)                   ENDOFJOB
021750,000042:                                                                                                  #    R22LEM  (DATA READ)                      GOPERF1
021751,000043:                                                                                                  #    R31LEM  (RENDEZVOUS PARAMETER DISPLAY)    
021752,000044:                                                                                                  #    PRIOLARM (PRIORITY DISPLAY)
021753,000045:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES-
021754,000046:                                                                                                  #    P20 MAY BE TERMINATED IN TWO WAYS-ASTRONAUT SELECTION OF IDLING
021755,000047:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM (P00) BY KEYING V37E00E OR BY KEYING IN V56E
021756,000048:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES-
021757,000049:                                                                                                  #    RANGE GREATER THAN 400 NM DISPLAY
021758,000050:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
021759,000051:                                                                                                  #    TRKMKCNT = NO OF RENDEZVOUS TRACKING MARKS TAKEN (COUNTER)
021760,000052:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
021761,000053:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
021762,000054:                                                                                                  #    SRCHOPT,RNDVZFLG,ACMODFLG,VEHUPFLG,UPDATFLG,TRACKFLG,
021763,000055:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
021764,000056:                                                                                                  #    CENTRALS-A,Q,L
021765,000057: 25,2053  30,2000                                  SBANK=   LOWSUPER                              #  FOR LOW 2CADR'S.
021766,000058: 
021767,000059: 33,2117                                           BANK     33                                    
021768,000060: 24,2000                                           SETLOC   P20S                                  
021769,000061: 24,2000                                           BANK                                           
021770,000062: 
021771,000063: 24,2000  E7,1456                                  EBANK=   LOSCOUNT                              
021772,000064: 24,2000                                           COUNT*   $$/P20                                
021773,000065: 24,2000  24,2000               PROG22             =        PROG20                                
021774,000066: 24,2000           05340        PROG20             TC       2PHSCHNG                              
021775,000067: 24,2001           00004                           OCT      4

022254,000546:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
022255,000547:                                                                                                  #  PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE PROGRAM P25
022256,000548:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 3
022257,000549:                                                                                                  #  BY  P. VOLANTE
022258,000550:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
022259,000551: 
022260,000552:                                                                                                  #    THE PURPOSE OF THIS PROGRAM IS TO COMPUTE THE PREFERRED TRACKING
022261,000553:                                                                                                  #  ATTITUDE OF THE LM TO CONTINUOUSLY POINT THE LM TRACKING BEACON AT THE
022262,000554:                                                                                                  #  CSM AND TO PERFORM THE MANEUVER TO THE PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE AND
022263,000555:                                                                                                  #  CONTINUOUSLY MAINTAIN THIS ATTITUDE WITHIN PRESCRIBED LIMITS
022264,000556:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
022265,000557:                                                                                                  #    ASTRONAUT REQUEST THROUGH DSKY V37E25E
022266,000558:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED -
022267,000559:                                                                                                  #    BANKCALL                      FLAGUP
022268,000560:                                                                                                  #    R02BOTH  (IMU STATUS CHECK)   ENDOFJOB
022269,000561:                                                                                                  #    R61LEM   (PREF TRK ATT ROUT)  WAITLIST
022270,000562:                                                                                                  #    TASKOVER                      FINDVAC
022271,000563:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES  -
022272,000564:                                                                                                  #    P25 MAY BE TERMINATED IN TWO WAYS-ASTRONAUT SELECTION OF IDLING
022273,000565:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM(P00) BY KEYING V37E00E OR BY KEYING IN V56E
022274,000566:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
022275,000567:                                                                                                  #    NONE
022276,000568:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
022277,000569:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
022278,000570:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
022279,000571:                                                                                                  #    TRACKFLG,P25FLAG
022280,000572:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
022281,000573:                                                                                                  #    NONE
022282,000574: 24,2462  E7,1456                                  EBANK=   LOSCOUNT                              
022283,000575: 24,2462                                           COUNT*   $$/P25                                
022284,000576: 24,2462           05340        PROG25             TC       2PHSCHNG                              
022285,000577: 24,2463           00004                           OCT      4                                     #  MAKE GROUP 4 INACTIVE (VERB 37)
022286,000578: 24,2464           05022                           OCT      05022                                 
022287,000579: 24,2465           26000                           OCT      26000                                 #  PRIORITY 26
022288,000580: 
022289,000581: 24,2466           04616                           TC       BANKCALL                              
022290,000582: 24,2467           11241                           CADR     R02BOTH                               #  IMU STATUS CHECK
022291,000583: 24,2470           05515                           TC       UPFLAG                                
022292,000584: 24,2471           00031                           ADRES    TRACKFLG                              #  SET TRACK FLAG
022293,000585: 24,2472           05515                           TC       UPFLAG

022305,000597: 24,2505           70075                           MASK     STATE      +1

022326,000618:                                                                                                  #  DATA READ ROUTINE 22 (LEM)
022327,000619:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
022328,000620:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 2
022329,000621:                                                                                                  #  BY P VOLANTE
022330,000622:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
022331,000623: 
022332,000624:                                                                                                  #    TO PROCESS AUTOMATIC RR MARK DATA TO UPDATE THE STATE VECTOR OF EITHER
022333,000625:                                                                                                  #  LM OR CSM AS DEFINED IN THE RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION PROGRAM (P20)
022334,000626:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
022335,000627:                                                                                                  #           TC     BANKCALL
022336,000628:                                                                                                  #           CADR   R22LEM
022337,000629:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED -
022338,000630:                                                                                                  #    LSR22.1           GOFLASH        WAITLIST
022339,000631:                                                                                                  #    LSR22.2           PRIOLARM       BANKCALL
022340,000632:                                                                                                  #    LSR22.3           R61LEM
022341,000633:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES-
022342,000634:                                                                                                  #    R22 WILL CONTINUE TO RECYCLE,UPDATING STATE VECTORS WITH RADAR DATA
022343,000635:                                                                                                  #  UNTIL P20 CEASES TO OPERATE (RENDEZVOUS FLAG SET TO ZERO) AT WHICH TIME
022344,000636:                                                                                                  #  R22 WILL TERMINATE SELF.
022345,000637:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES-
022346,000638:                                                                                                  #    PRIORITY ALARM
022347,000639:                                                                                                  #  PRIORITY ALARM 525 LOS NOT WITHIN 3 DEGREE LIMIT
022348,000640:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
022349,000641:                                                                                                  #    SEE OUTPUT FROM LSR22.3
022350,000642:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
022351,000643:                                                                                                  #    SEE LSR22.1,LSR22.2,LSR22.3
022352,000644:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
022353,000645:                                                                                                  #    NOANGFLG
022354,000646:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
022355,000647:                                                                                                  #    SEE LSR22.1,LSR22.2,LSR22.3
022356,000648: 24,2527  E7,1737                                  EBANK=   LRS22.1X

022530,000822:                                                                                                  #  RR DESIGNATE ROUTINE (R21LEM)
022531,000823:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
022532,000824:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 2
022533,000825:                                                                                                  #  BY P VOLANTE
022534,000826:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
022535,000827: 
022536,000828:                                                                                                  #    TO POINT THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR AT THE CSM UNTIL AUTOMATIC ACQUISITION
022537,000829:                                                                                                  #  OF THE CSM IS ACCOMPLISHED BY THE RADAR. ROUTINE IS CALLED BY P20.
022538,000830:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
022539,000831:                                                                                                  #           TC     BANKCALL
022540,000832:                                                                                                  #           CADR   R21LEM
022541,000833:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED -
022542,000834:                                                                                                  #    FINDVAC        FLAGUP           ENDOFJOB        PRIOLARM
022543,000835:                                                                                                  #    NOVAC          INTPRET          LPS20.1         PHASCHNG
022544,000836:                                                                                                  #    WAITLIST       JOBSLEEP         JOBWAKE         FLAGDOWN
022545,000837:                                                                                                  #    TASKOVER       BANKCALL         RADSTALL        RRDESSM
022546,000838:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES
022547,000839:                                                                                                  #    WHEN LOCK-ON IS ACHIEVED,BRANCH WILL BE TO P20 WHERE R22 (DATA READ
022548,000840:                                                                                                  #  WILL BE SELECTED OR A NEED FOR A MANEUVER(BRANCH TO P20LEMA)
022549,000841:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES-
022550,000842:                                                                                                  #    PRIORITY ALARM 503 WHEN LOCK-ON HASN:T BEEN ACHIEVED AFTER 30SECS -
022551,000843:                                                                                                  #  THIS REQUIRES ASTRONAUT INTERFACE- SELECTION OF SEARCH OPTION OF
022552,000844:                                                                                                  #  ACQUISITION
022553,000845:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
022554,000846:                                                                                                  #    SEE LPS20.1,RRDESSM
022555,000847:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
022556,000848:                                                                                                  #    RRTARGET,RADMODES ARE USED BY LPS20.1 AND RRDESSM
022557,000849:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
022558,000850:                                                                                                  #    LOSCMFLG      LOKONSW
022559,000851:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
022560,000852:                                                                                                  #    SEE LPS20.1,RRDESSM

022736,001028:                                                                                                  #  MANUAL ACQUISITION ROUTINE R23LEM
022737,001029:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
022738,001030:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 2
022739,001031:                                                                                                  #  BY P VOLANTE
022740,001032:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
022741,001033: 
022742,001034:                                                                                                  #    TO ACQUIRE THE CSM BY MANUAL OPERATION OF THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR
022743,001035:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
022744,001036:                                                                                                  #           TC     R23LEM
022745,001037:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
022746,001038:                                                                                                  #    BANKCALL        R61LEM
022747,001039:                                                                                                  #    SETMINDB        GOPERF1
022748,001040:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES -
022749,001041:                                                                                                  #    IN RESPONSE TO THE GOPERF1 ,SELECTION OF ENTER WILL RECYCLE R23
022750,001042:                                                                                                  #                               ,SELECTION OF PROC  WILL CONTINUE R23
022751,001043:                                                                                                  #                               ,SELECTION OF TERM  WILL TERMINATE R23 +P20
022752,001044:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -

022806,001098:                                                                                                  #  SEARCH ROUTINE R24LEM
022807,001099:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
022808,001100:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 2
022809,001101:                                                                                                  #  BY  P. VOLANTE
022810,001102:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
022811,001103: 
022812,001104:                                                                                                  #    TO ACQUIRE THE CSM BY A SEARCH PATTERN WHEN THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR HAS
022813,001105:                                                                                                  #  FAILED TO ACQUIRE THE CSM IN THE AUTOMATIC TRACKING MODE AND TO ALLOW
022814,001106:                                                                                                  #  THE ASTRONAUT TO CONFIRM THAT REACQUISITION HAS NOT BEEN BY SIDELOBE.
022815,001107:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE
022816,001108:                                                                                                  #           CAF    PRIONN
022817,001109:                                                                                                  #           TC     FINDVAC
022818,001110:                                                                                                  #           EBANK= DATAGOOD
022819,001111:                                                                                                  #           2CADR  R24LEM
022820,001112:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
022821,001113:                                                                                                  #    FLAGUP        FLAGDOWN      BANKCALL
022822,001114:                                                                                                  #    R61LEM        GOFLASHR      FINDVAC
022823,001115:                                                                                                  #    ENDOFJOB      NOVAC         LSR24.1
022824,001116:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES-
022825,001117:                                                                                                  #    ASTRONAUT RESPONSE TO DISPLAY OF OMEGA AND DATAGOOD.HE CAN EITHER
022826,001118:                                                                                                  #  REJECT BY TERMINATING (SEARCH OPTION AND RESELECTING P20) OR ACCEPT BY
022827,001119:                                                                                                  #  PROCEEDING (EXIT ROUTINE AND RETURN TO AUTO MODE IN P20)
022828,001120:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES-
022829,001121:                                                                                                  #    SEE NORMAL EXIT MODES ABOVE
022830,001122:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT -
022831,001123:                                                                                                  #    SEE OUTPUT FROM LSR24.1 + R61LEM
022832,001124:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
022833,001125:                                                                                                  #    SEE INPUT FOR LSR24.1
022834,001126:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
022835,001127:                                                                                                  #    SRCHOPT,ACMODFLG
022836,001128: 24,3272  E7,1733                                  EBANK=   DATAGOOD                              
022837,001129: 24,3272                                           COUNT*   $$/R24                                
022838,001130: 24,3272           05515        R24LEM             TC       UPFLAG                                
022839,001131: 24,3273           00037                           ADRES    SRCHOPTN                              #  SET SRCHOPT FLAG
022840,001132: 24,3274           05527                           TC       DOWNFLAG                              #  RESET LOS BEING COMPUTED FLAG TO MAKE
022841,001133: 24,3275           00041                           ADRES    LOSCMFLG                              #  SURE DODES DOESN'T GO TO R21
022842,001134: 24,3276           34755        R24LEM1            CAF      ZERO

022907,001199:                                                                                                  #  PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE ROUTINE R61LEM
022908,001200:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
022909,001201:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO : 3                      DATE : 4-11-67
022910,001202:                                                                                                  #  MOD BY : P VOLANTE  SDC
022911,001203: 
022912,001204: 
022913,001205:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION-
022914,001206:                                                                                                  #    TO COMPUTE THE PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE OF THE LM TO ENABLE RR
022915,001207:                                                                                                  #  TRACKING OF THE CSM AND TO PERFORM THE MANEUVER TO THE PREFERRED
022916,001208:                                                                                                  #  ATTITUDE.

023116,001408:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRLIMCHK                                                  ARE IN THE LIMITS OF THE CURRENT MODE.
023117,001409: 
023118,001410:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023119,001411:                                                                                                  #  RRLIMCHK CHECKS RR DESIRED GIMBAL ANGLES TO SEE IF THEY ARE WITHIN
023120,001412:                                                                                                  #  THE LIMITS OF THE CURRENT MODE. INITIALLY THE DESIRED TRUNNION AND
023121,001413:                                                                                                  #  SHAFT ANGLES ARE STORED IN ITEMP1 AND ITEMP2. THE CURRENT RR
023122,001414:                                                                                                  #  ANTENNAE MODE (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED WHICH IS = 0 FOR
023123,001415:                                                                                                  #  MODE 1 AND =1 FOR MODE 2.
023124,001416:                                                                                                  #  MODE 1 - THE TRUNNION ANGLE IS CHECKED AT MAGSUB TO SEE IF IT IS
023125,001417:                                                                                                  #  BETWEEN -55 AND +55 DEGREES. IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2. IF WITHIN LIMITS,
023126,001418:                                                                                                  #  THE SHAFT ANGLE IS CHECKED TO SEE IF IT IS BETWEEN -70 AND +59 DEGREES.
023127,001419:                                                                                                  #  IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2. IF IN LIMITS, RETURN TO L +3.
023128,001420:                                                                                                  #  MODE 2 - THE SHAFT ANGLE IS CHECKED AT MAGSUB TO SEE IF IT IS
023129,001421:                                                                                                  #  BETWEEN -139 AND -25 DEGREES. IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2. IF WITHIN
023130,001422:                                                                                                  #  LIMITS, THE TRUNNION ANGLE IS CHECKED TO SEE IF IT IS BETWEEN +125
023131,001423:                                                                                                  #  AND -125 (+235) DEGREES. IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2. IF IN LIMITS, RETURN
023132,001424:                                                                                                  #  TO L +3.
023133,001425: 
023134,001426:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023135,001427:                                                                                                  #  L  TC  RRLIMCHK (WITH INTERRUPT INHIBITED)
023136,001428:                                                                                                  #  L +1  ADRES T,S   (DESIRED TRUNNION ANGLE ADDRESS)
023137,001429: 
023138,001430:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023139,001431:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES, MODEA, MODEB (OR DESIRED TRUNNION AND SHAFT
023140,001432:                                                                                                  #  ANGLES ELSEWHERE IN CONSECUTIVE LOCATIONS - UNSWITCHED ERASABLE OR
023141,001433:                                                                                                  #  CURRENT EBANK).
023142,001434: 
023143,001435:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_  MAGSUB
023144,001436: 
023145,001437:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_  NONE
023146,001438: 
023147,001439:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
023148,001440: 
023149,001441:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  L + 2 (EITHER OR BOTH ANGLES NOT WITHIN LIMITS OF CURRENT MODE)
023150,001442:                                                                                                  #  L + 3 (BOTH ANGLES WITHIN LIMITS OF CURRENT MODE)
023151,001443:

023195,001487:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  SETTRKF                                                  . IF EITHER:
023196,001488: 
023197,001489:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023198,001490:                                                                                                  #  SETTRKF UPDATES THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP ON THE DSKY.                      HER THE ALT OR VEL INFORMATION.
023199,001491:                                                                                                  #  INITIALLY THE LAMP TEST FLAG (IMODES33 BIT 1) IS CHECKED.
023200,001492:                                                                                                  #  IF A LAMP TEST IS IN PROGRESS, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L +1.
023201,001493:                                                                                                  #  IF NO LAMP TEST THE FOLLOWING IS CHECKED SEQUENTIALLY_
023202,001494:                                                                                                  #  1) RR CDU:S BEING ZEROED, RR CDU OK, AND RR NOT IN
023203,001495:                                                                                                  #  AUTO MODE (RADMODES BITS 13, 7, 2).
023204,001496:                                                                                                  #  2) LR VEL DATA FAIL AND NO LR POS DATA (RADMODES BITS
023205,001497:                                                                                                  #  8,5)
023206,001498:                                                                                                  #  3) NO RR DATA (RADMODES BIT 4)
023207,001499:                                                                                                  #  THE ABSENCE OF ALL THREE SIMULTANEOUSLY IN (1), THE PRESENCE OF BOTH
023208,001500:                                                                                                  #  IN (2), AND THE PRESENCE OF (3) RESULTS IN EITHER THE TRACKER FAIL
023209,001501:                                                                                                  #  LAMP (DSPTAB +11D BIT 8) BEING TURNED ON OR LEFT ON. OTHERWISE,
023210,001502:                                                                                                  #  THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP IS TURNED OFF OR IS LEFT OFF. THEREFORE, THE
023211,001503:                                                                                                  #  TRACKER FAIL LAMP IS TURNED ON IF_
023212,001504:                                                                                                  #  A ) RR CDU FAILED WITH RR IN AUTO MODE AND RR CDU:S NOT BEING ZEROED.
023213,001505:                                                                                                  #  B) N SAMPLES OF LR DATA COULD NOT BE TAKEN IN 2N TRIES WITH
023214,001506:                                                                                                  #  EITHER THE ALT OR VEL INFORMATION
023215,001507:                                                                                                  #  C) N SAMPLES OF RR DATA COULD NOT BE OBTAINED FROM 2N TRIES
023216,001508:                                                                                                  #  WITH EITHER THE AL
023217,001509: 
023218,001510:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023219,001511:                                                                                                  #  L  TC  SETTRKF
023220,001512: 
023221,001513:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED: IMODES33, RADMODES, DSPTAB +11D
023222,001514:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_  NONE
023223,001515: 
023224,001516:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_  NONE
023225,001517: 
023226,001518:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  TRACKER FAIL LAMP
023227,001519: 
023228,001520:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  L +1 (ALWAYS)                                                         ED.
023229,001521:

023265,001557:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRTURNON
023266,001558: 
023267,001559:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023268,001560: 
023269,001561:                                                                                                  #  RRTURNON IS THE TURN-ON SEQUENCE WHICH, ALONG WITH
023270,001562:                                                                                                  #  RRZEROSB, ZEROS THE CDU:S AND DETERMINES THE RR MODE.
023271,001563:                                                                                                  #  INITIALLY, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO RRZEROSB FOR THE
023272,001564:                                                                                                  #  ACTUAL TURN-ON SEQUENCE. UPON RETURN THE PROGRAM
023273,001565:                                                                                                  #  WAITS 1 SECOND BEFORE REMOVING THE TURN-ON FLAG
023274,001566:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT1) SO THE REPOSITION ROUTINE WON:T
023275,001567:                                                                                                  #  INITIATE PROGRAM ALARM 00501. A CHECK IS THEN MADE
023276,001568:                                                                                                  #  TO SEE IF A PROGRAM IS USING THE RR (STATE BIT 7). IF
023277,001569:                                                                                                  #  SO, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO ENDRADAR SO THAT THE RR CDU
023278,001570:                                                                                                  #  FAIL FLAG (RADMODES BIT 7) CAN BE CHECKED BEFORE
023279,001571:                                                                                                  #  RETURNING TO THE WAITING PROGRAM. IF NOT, THE PROGRAM EXITS
023280,001572:                                                                                                  #  TO TASKOVER.
023281,001573: 
023282,001574:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE: WAITLIST TASK FROM RRAUTCHK IF THE RR POWER ON AUTO
023283,001575:                                                                                                  #  BIT (CHAN 33 BIT 2) CHANGES TO 0 AND NO PROGRAM WAS USING 
023284,001576:                                                                                                  #  THE RR (STATE BIT 7).
023285,001577: 
023286,001578:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023287,001579:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES, STATE
023288,001580: 
023289,001581:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_  RRZEROSB, FIXDELAY, TASKOVER, ENDRADAR
023290,001582: 
023291,001583:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
023292,001584:                                                                                                  #  NONE
023293,001585: 
023294,001586:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE (SEE RRZEROSB)
023295,001587: 
023296,001588:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  TASKOVER, ENDRADAR (WAITING PROGRAM)
023297,001589: 
023298,001590: 24,3340                                           BANK     24                                    
023299,001591: 25,2000                                           SETLOC   P20S1                                 
023300,001592: 25,2000                                           BANK                                           
023301,001593: 
023302,001594: 25,2053  E7,1456                                  EBANK=   LOSCOUNT                              
023303,001595: 25,2053                                           COUNT*   $$/RSUB                               
023304,001596: 25,2053           02062        RRTURNON           TC       RRZEROSB                              
023305,001597: 25,2054           05232                           TC       FIXDELAY                              #  WAIT 1 SEC BEFORE REMOVING TURN ON FLAG
023306,001598: 25,2055           00144                           DEC      100        B-14                       #  SO A MONITOR REPOSITION WONT ALARM.

023313,001605:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRZEROSB
023314,001606: 
023315,001607:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023316,001608:                                                                                                  #  RRZEROSB IS A CLOSED SUBROUTINE TO ZERO THE RR CDU:S,
023317,001609:                                                                                                  #  DETERMINE THE RR MODE, AND TURNS ON THE TRACKER FAIL
023318,001610:                                                                                                  #  LAMP IF REQUIRED. INITIALLY THE RR CDU ZERO BIT (CHAN 12
023319,001611:                                                                                                  #  BIT 1) IS SET. FOLLOWING A 20 MILLISECOND WAIT, THE LGC
023320,001612:                                                                                                  #  RR CDU COUNTERS (OPTY, OPTX) ARE SET = 0 AFTER 
023321,001613:                                                                                                  #  WHICH THE RR CDU ZERO DISCRETE (CHAN 12 BIT 1) IS
023322,001614:                                                                                                  #  REMOVED. A 4 SECOND WAIT IS SET TO ALL THE RR CDU:S
023323,001615:                                                                                                  #  TO REPEAT THE ACTUAL TRUNNION AND SHAFT ANGLES. THE
023324,001616:                                                                                                  #  RR CDU ZERO FLAG (RADMODES BIT 13) IS REMOVED. THE
023325,001617:                                                                                                  #  CONTENTS OF OPTY IS THEN CHECKED TO SEE IF THE TRUNNION
023326,001618:                                                                                                  #  ANGLE IS LESS THAN 90 DEGREES. IF NOT, BIT 12 OF
023327,001619:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES IS SET = 1 TO INDICATE RR ANTENNA MODE 2.
023328,001620:                                                                                                  #  IF LESS THAN 90 DEGREES, BIT 12 OF RADMODES IS SET = 0 TO
023329,001621:                                                                                                  #  INDICATE RR ANTENNA MODE 1. SETTRKF IS THEN CALLED TO
023330,001622:                                                                                                  #  SEE IF THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP SHOULD BE TURNED ON.
023331,001623: 
023332,001624:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE: L  TC  RRZEROSB (FROM RRTURNON AND RRZERO)
023333,001625:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023334,001626:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES (BIT 13 SET), DSPTAB +11D
023335,001627: 
023336,001628:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_  FIXDELAY, MAGSUB, SETTRKF
023337,001629: 
023338,001630:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
023339,001631:                                                                                                  #  NONE
023340,001632: 
023341,001633:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  TRACKER FAIL
023342,001634: 
023343,001635:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  L +1 (ALWAYS)
023344,001636: 
023345,001637: 25,2062           00006        RRZEROSB           EXTEND                                         
023346,001638: 25,2063           23312                           QXCH     RRRET                                 
023347,001639: 25,2064           34753                           CAF      BIT1                                  #  BIT 13 OF RADMODES MUST BE SET BEFORE
023348,001640: 25,2065           00006                           EXTEND                                         #  COMING HERE.
023349,001641: 25,2066           05012                           WOR      CHAN12                                #  TURN ON ZERO RR CDU
023350,001642: 25,2067           05232                           TC       FIXDELAY                              
023351,001643: 25,2070           00002                           DEC      2          B-14                       
023352,001644:

023355,001647: 25,2073           54036                           TS       CDUS

023357,001649: 25,2075           00006                           EXTEND

023386,001678:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  DORREPOS
023387,001679:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023388,001680:                                                                                                  #  DORREPOS IS A SEQUENCE OF TASKS TO DRIVE THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR
023389,001681:                                                                                                  #  TO A SAFE POSITION. INITIALLY SETRRECR IS CALLED WHERE THE RR
023390,001682:                                                                                                  #  ERROR COUNTERS (CHAN 12 BIT 2) ARE ENABLED AND LASTYCMD
023391,001683:                                                                                                  #  AND LASTXCMD SET = 0 TO INDICATE THE DIFFERENCE BETWEEN THE
023392,001684:                                                                                                  #  DESIRED STATE AND PRESENT STATE OF THE COMMANDS. THE RR
023393,001685:                                                                                                  #  TURN-ON FLAG (RADMODES BIT 1) IS CHECKED AND IF NOT PRESENT,
023394,001686:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM ALARM 00501 IS REQUESTED BEFORE CONTINUING. IN EITHER
023395,001687:                                                                                                  #  CASE, FOLLOWING A 20 MILLISECOND WAIT THE PROGRAM CHECKS THE CURRENT
023396,001688:                                                                                                  #  RR ANTENNA MODE (RADMODES BIT 12). RRTONLY IS THEN CALLED
023397,001689:                                                                                                  #  TO DRIVE THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1 AND TO 180
023398,001690:                                                                                                  #  DEGREES IF IN MODE 2. UPON RETURN, THE CURRENT RR ANTENNA
023399,001691:                                                                                                  #  MODE (RADMODES BIT 12) IS AGAIN CHECKED. RRSONLY IS THEN
023400,001692:                                                                                                  #  CALLED TO DRIVE THE SHAFT ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1 AND TO
023401,001693:                                                                                                  #  -90 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2. IF DURING RRTONLY OR RRSONLY A
023402,001694:                                                                                                  #  REMODE HAS BEEN REQUESTED (RADMODES BIT 14), AND ALWAYS
023403,001695:                                                                                                  #  FOLLOWING COMPLETION OF RRSONLY, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO
023404,001696:                                                                                                  #  REPOSRPT. HERE THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS 
023405,001697:                                                                                                  #  REMOVED. A CHECK IS THEN MADE ON THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
023406,001698:                                                                                                  #  BIT 10). IF PRESENT, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO BEGDES. IF NOT PRESENT
023407,001699:                                                                                                  #  INDICATING NO FURTHER ANTENNA CONTROL REQUIRED, THE RR ERROR
023408,001700:                                                                                                  #  COUNTER BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2) IS REMOVED AND THE ROUTINE EXITS TO
023409,001701:                                                                                                  #  TASKOVER.
023410,001702: 
023411,001703:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023412,001704:                                                                                                  #  WAITLIST CALL FROM RRGIMON IF TRUNNION AND SHAFT CDU ANGLES
023413,001705:                                                                                                  #  NOT WITHIN LIMITS OF CURRENT MODE.
023414,001706: 
023415,001707:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023416,001708:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES
023417,001709: 
023418,001710:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
023419,001711:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY, RRSONLY, BEGDES (EXIT)
023420,001712: 
023421,001713:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
023422,001714:                                                                                                  #  NONE
023423,001715: 
023424,001716:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS-  NONE
023425,001717: 
023426,001718:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  TASKOVER, BEGDES
023427,001719: 
023428,001720: 25,2120           02147        DORREPOS           TC       SETRRECR                              #  SET UP RR CDU ERROR COUNTERS.

023473,001765:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  REMODE                                                   IVES SHAFT TO -45, AND FINALLY DRIVES
023474,001766: 
023475,001767:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_                                                 S DONE WITH SINGLE AXIS ROTATIONS (SEE
023476,001768:                                                                                                  #  REMODE IS THE GENERAL REMODING SUBROUTINE. IT DRIVES THE
023477,001769:                                                                                                  #  TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF THE CURRENT MODE IS MODE 1,
023478,001770:                                                                                                  #  180 DEGREES FOR MODE 2, THEN DRIVES THE SHAFT ANGLE TO -45
023479,001771:                                                                                                  #  DEGREES, AND FINALLY DRIVES THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO -130 DEGREES,
023480,001772:                                                                                                  #  TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 2, -50 DEGREES FOR MODE 1, BEFORE
023481,001773:                                                                                                  #  INITIATING 2-AXIS CONTROL. ALL REMODING IS DONE WITH SINGLE
023482,001774:                                                                                                  #  AXIS ROTATIONS (RR1AXIS). INITIALLY THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG
023483,001775:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED. CONTROL IS THEN TRANSFERRED TO
023484,001776:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY TO DRIVE THR TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1
023485,001777:                                                                                                  #  OR 180 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2. RRSONLY IS THEN CALLED TO DRIVE
023486,001778:                                                                                                  #  THE SHAFT ANGLE TO -45 DEGREES. THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG
023487,001779:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED AGAIN. CONTROL IS AGAIN
023488,001780:                                                                                                  #  TRANSFERRED TO RRTONLY TO DRIVE THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO -130
023489,001781:                                                                                                  #  DEGREES TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 2 IF CURRENTLY IN MODE 1 OR TO
023490,001782:                                                                                                  #  -50 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2 TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 1. RMODINV
023491,001783:                                                                                                  #  IS THEN CALLED TO SET RADMODES BIT 12 TO INDICATE THE NEW
023492,001784:                                                                                                  #  RR ANTENNA MODE. THE REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14)
023493,001785:                                                                                                  #  IS REMOVED TO INDICATE THAT REMODING IS COMPLETE. THE PROGRAM
023494,001786:                                                                                                  #  THEN EXITS TO STDESIG TO BEGIN 2-AXIS CONTROL.
023495,001787: 
023496,001788:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023497,001789:                                                                                                  #  FROM BEGDES WHEN REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14) IS SET.
023498,001790:                                                                                                  #  THIS FLAG MAY BE SET IN RRDESSM AND RRDESNB IF RRLIMCHK
023499,001791:                                                                                                  #  DETERMINES THAT THE DESIRED ANGLES ARE WITHIN THE LIMITS OF THE
023500,001792:                                                                                                  #  OTHER MODE.
023501,001793: 
023502,001794:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023503,001795:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES
023504,001796: 
023505,001797:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
023506,001798:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY, RRSONLY, RMODINV (ACTUALLY PART OF)
023507,001799: 
023508,001800:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
023509,001801:                                                                                                  #  NONE
023510,001802: 
023511,001803:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE

023566,001858:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAMES_  RRTONLY, RRSONLY
023567,001859: 
023568,001860:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023569,001861:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY AND RRSONLY ARE SUBROUTINES FOR DOING SINGLE AXIS
023570,001862:                                                                                                  #  RR MANEUVERS FOR REMODE AND REPOSITION. IT DRIVES TO
023571,001863:                                                                                                  #  WITHIN 1 DEGREE. INITIALLY, AT RR1AX2, THE REMODE AND REPOSITION
023572,001864:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS (RADMODES BITS 14, 11) ARE CHECKED. IF BOTH EXIST,
023573,001865:                                                                                                  #  THE PROGRAM EXITS TO REPOSRPT (SEE DORREPOS). THIS INDICATES
023574,001866:                                                                                                  #  THAT SOMEONE POSSIBLY REQUESTED A DESIGNATE (RADMODES BIT 10)
023575,001867:                                                                                                  #  WHICH REQUIRES A REMODE (RADMODES BIT 14) AND THAT A
023576,001868:                                                                                                  #  REPOSITION IS IN PROGRESS (RADMODES BIT 11). IF NONE
023577,001869:                                                                                                  #  OR ONLY ONE OF THE FLAGS EXIST, REMODE OR REPOSITION, MAGSUB
023578,001870:                                                                                                  #  IS CALLED TO SEE IF THE APPROPRIATE ANGLE IS WITHIN 1 DEGREE. IF YES,
023579,001871:                                                                                                  #  CONTROL RETURNS TO THE CALLING ROUTINE. IF NOT, CONTROL IS
023580,001872:                                                                                                  #  TRANSFERRED TO RROUT FOR SINGLE AXIS MANEUVERS WITH THE OTHER
023581,001873:                                                                                                  #  ANGLE SET = 0. FOLLOWING A .5 SECOND WAIT, THE ABOVE PROCEDURE IS
023582,001874:                                                                                                  #  REPEATED.
023583,001875: 
023584,001876:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE: L-1 CAF *ANGLE*  (DESIRED ANGLE SCALED PI)
023585,001877:                                                                                                  #  L  TC  RRTONLY (TRUNNION ONLY)
023586,001878:                                                                                                  #  RRSONLY (SHAFT ONLY)
023587,001879:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY IS CALLED BY PREPOS29;
023588,001880:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY AND RRSONLY ARE CALLED BY DORREPOS AND REMODE
023589,001881: 
023590,001882:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023591,001883:                                                                                                  #  C(A) = DESIRED ANGLE, RADMODES
023592,001884: 
023593,001885:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
023594,001886:                                                                                                  #  FIXDELAY, REPOSRPT, MAGSUB, RROUT
023595,001887: 
023596,001888:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
023597,001889:                                                                                                  #  NONE
023598,001890: 
023599,001891:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
023600,001892: 
023601,001893:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  REPOSRPT (REMODE AND REPOSITION FLAGS PRESENT - RADMODES
023602,001894:                                                                                                  #  BITS 14, 11)
023603,001895:                                                                                                  #  L+1  (ANGLE WITHIN ONE DEGREE OR RR OUT OF AUTO MODE)
023604,001896:

023654,001946:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RROUT                                                    RROR COUNTER SCALING. RROUT LIMITS THEM
023655,001947: 
023656,001948:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023657,001949:                                                                                                  #  RROUT RECEIVES RR GYRO COMMANDS IN TANG, TANG +1 IN RR
023658,001950:                                                                                                  #  ERROR COUNTER SCALING. RROUT THEN LIMITS THEM AND
023659,001951:                                                                                                  #  GENERATES COMMANDS TO THE CDU TO ADJUST THE ERROR COUNTERS
023660,001952:                                                                                                  #  TO THE DESIRED VALUES. INITIALLY MAGSUB CHECKS THE MAGNITUDE OF
023661,001953:                                                                                                  #  THE COMMAND (SHAFT ON 1ST PASS) TO SEE IF IT IS GREATER THAN
023662,001954:                                                                                                  #  384 PULSES. IF NOT, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO RROUTLIM TO
023663,001955:                                                                                                  #  LIMIT THE COMMAND TO +384 OR -384 PULSES. THE DIFFERENCE IS
023664,001956:                                                                                                  #  THEN CALCULATED BETWEEN THE DESIRED STATE AND THE PRESENT STATE OF
023665,001957:                                                                                                  #  THE ERROR COUNTER AS RECORDED IN LASTYCMD AND LASTXCMD.
023666,001958:                                                                                                  #  THE RESULT IS STORED IN OPTXCMD (1ST PASS) AND OPTYCMD (2ND
023667,001959:                                                                                                  #  PASS). FOLLOWING THE SECOND PASS, FOR THE TRUNNION COMMAND, THE
023668,001960:                                                                                                  #  OCDUT AND OCDUS ERROR COUNTER DRIVE BITS (CHAN 14 BITS 12, 11)
023669,001961:                                                                                                  #  ARE SET. THIS PROGRAM THEN EXITS TO THE CALLING PROGRAM.
023670,001962: 
023671,001963:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023672,001964:                                                                                                  #  L TC RROUT (WITH RUPT INHIBITED) RROUT IS CALLED BY
023673,001965:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY, RRSONLY, AND DODES
023674,001966: 
023675,001967:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023676,001968:                                                                                                  #  TANG, TANG +1 (DESIRED COMMANDS), LASTYCMD, LASTXCMD
023677,001969:                                                                                                  #  (1ST PASS = 0), RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE SET (CHAN 12 BIT 2).

023760,002052:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRDESSM                                                  R (HALF-UNIT) IN RRTARGET. REMODES IF
023761,002053: 
023762,002054:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023763,002055:                                                                                                  #  THIS INTERPRETIVE ROUTINE WILL DESIGNATE, IF DESIRED ANGLES ARE
023764,002056:                                                                                                  #  WITHIN THE LIMITS OF EITHER MODE, TO A LINE-OF SIGHT (LOS) VECTOR
023765,002057:                                                                                                  #  (HALF-UNIT) KNOWN WITH RESPECT TO THE STABLE MEMBER PRESENT
023766,002058:                                                                                                  #  ORIENTATION. INITIALLY THE IMU CDU:S ARE READ AND CONTROL
023767,002059:                                                                                                  #  TRANSFERRED TO SMNB TO TRANSFORM THE LOS VECTOR FROM STABLE
023768,002060:                                                                                                  #  MEMBER TO NAVIGATION BASE COORDINATES (SEE STG MEMO -699)
023769,002061:                                                                                                  #  RRANGLES IS THEN CALLED TO CALCULATE THE RR GIMBAL ANGLES,
023770,002062:                                                                                                  #  TRUNNION AND SHAFT, FOR BOTH THE PRESENT AND ALTERNATE MODE.
023771,002063:                                                                                                  #  RRLIMCHK IS CALLED TO SEE IF THE ANGLES CALCULATED FOR THE
023772,002064:                                                                                                  #  PRESENT MODE ARE WITHIN LIMITS. IF WITHIN LIMITS, THE RETURN
023773,002065:                                                                                                  #  LOCATION IS INCREMENTED, INASMUCH AS NO VEHICLE MANEUVER IS
023774,002066:                                                                                                  #  REQUIRED, BEFORE EXITING TO STARTDES. IF NOT WITHIN LIMITS OF THE
023775,002067:                                                                                                  #  CURRENT MODE, TRYSWS IS CALLED. FOLLOWING INVERTING OF THE RR
023776,002068:                                                                                                  #  ANTENNA MODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 12), RRLIMCHK IS CALLED
023777,002069:                                                                                                  #  TO SEE IF THE ANGLES CALCULATED FOR THE ALTERNATE MODE ARE WITHIN
023778,002070:                                                                                                  #  LIMITS. IF YES, THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG IS AGAIN INVERTED,
023779,002071:                                                                                                  #  THE REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14) SET, AND THE RETURN LOCATION
023780,002072:                                                                                                  #  INCREMENTED, TO INDICATE NO VEHICLE MANEUVER IS REQUIRED, BEFORE
023781,002073:                                                                                                  #  EXITING TO STARTDES. IF THESE ANGLES ARE NOT WITHIN LIMITS
023782,002074:                                                                                                  #  OF THE ALTERNATE MODE, THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG (RADMODES
023783,002075:                                                                                                  #  BIT 12) IS INVERTED BEFORE RETURNING DIRECTLY TO THE CALLING PROGRAM
023784,002076:                                                                                                  #  TO INDICATE THAT A VEHICLE MANEUVER IS REQUIRED.
023785,002077: 
023786,002078:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023787,002079:                                                                                                  #  L  STCALL  RRTARGET  (LOS HALF-UNIT VECTOR IN SM COORDINATES)
023788,002080:                                                                                                  #  L+1  RRDESSM
023789,002081:                                                                                                  #  L+2  BASIC  (VEHICLE MANEUVER REQUIRED)
023790,002082:                                                                                                  #  L+3  BASIC  (NO VEHICLE MANEUVER REQUIRED)
023791,002083: 
023792,002084:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023793,002085:                                                                                                  #  RRTARGET, RADMODES
023794,002086: 
023795,002087:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
023796,002088:                                                                                                  #  READCDUS, SMNB, RRANGLES, RRLIMCHK, TRYSWS (ACTUALLY
023797,002089:                                                                                                  #  PART OF), RMODINV
023798,002090: 
023799,002091:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
023800,002092:                                                                                                  #  NONE
023801,002093: 
023802,002094:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
023803,002095: 
023804,002096:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  L+2 (NEITHER SET OF ANGLES ARE WITHIN LIMITS OF RELATED MODE)
023805,002097:                                                                                                  #  STARTDES (DESIGNATE POSSIBLE AT PRESENT VEHICLE ATTITUDE-RETURNS
023806,002098:                                                                                                  #  TO L+3 FROM STARTDES)                                                   CAN BE DONE IN PRESENT VEH ATTITUDE.
