023846,002138:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  STARTDES                                                 STORED AS A HALF-UNIT VECTOR IN RRTARGET
023847,002139: 
023848,002140:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_                                                 CKON IS DESIRED. BIT14 OF RADMODES IS
023849,002141:                                                                                                  #  STARTDES IS ENTERED WHEN WE ARE READY TO BEGIN DESIGNATION.             OR REPOSITION OPERATION. IN THIS
023850,002142:                                                                                                  #  BIT 14 OF RADMODES IS ALREADY SET IF A REMODE IS REQUIRED.              THE REPOSITION WILL BE INTERRUPTED.
023851,002143:                                                                                                  #  AT THIS TIME, THE RR ANTENNA MAY BE IN A REPOSITION                     GINS.
023852,002144:                                                                                                  #  OPERATION. IN THIS CASE, IF A REMODE IS REQUIRED IT MAY HAVE
023853,002145:                                                                                                  #  ALREADY BEGUN BUT IN ANY CASE THE REPOSITION WILL BE INTERRUPTED.
023854,002146:                                                                                                  #  OTHERWISE, THE REPOSITION WILL BE COMPLETED BEFORE 2-AXIS
023855,002147:                                                                                                  #  DESIGNATION BEGINS. INITIALLY DESCOUNT IS SET = 60 TO INDICATE
023856,002148:                                                                                                  #  THAT 30 SECONDS WILL BE ALLOWED FOR THE RR DATA GOOD INBIT
023857,002149:                                                                                                  #  (CHAN 33 BIT 4) IF LOCK-ON IS DESIRED (STATE BIT 5). BIT 10
023858,002150:                                                                                                  #  OF RADMODES IS SET TO SHOW THAT A DESIGNATE IS REQUIRED.
023859,002151:                                                                                                  #  THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS CHECKED. IF SET,
023860,002152:                                                                                                  #  THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L+3 OF THE CALLING PROGRAM (SEE RRDESSM
023861,002153:                                                                                                  #  AND RRDESNB). THE PROGRAM WILL BEGIN DESIGNATING TO THE DESIRED
023862,002154:                                                                                                  #  ANGLES FOLLOWING THE REPOSITION OR REMODE IF ONE WAS
023863,002155:                                                                                                  #  REQUESTED. IF THE REPOSITION FLAG IS NOT SET, SETRRECR IS CALLED
023864,002156:                                                                                                  #  WHICH SETS THE RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2)
023865,002157:                                                                                                  #  AND SETS LASTYCMD AND LASTXCMD = 0 TO INDICATE THE
023866,002158:                                                                                                  #  DIFFERENCE BETWEEN THE PRESENT AND DESIRED STATE OF THE ERROR
023867,002159:                                                                                                  #  COUNTERS. A 20 MILLISECOND WAITLIST CALL IS SET FOR BEGDES
023868,002160:                                                                                                  #  AFTER WHICH THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L+3 OF THE CALLING PROGRAM.
023869,002161:

024018,002310:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  BEGDES
024019,002311: 
024020,002312:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
024021,002313:                                                                                                  #  BEGDES CHECKS VARIOUS DESIGNATE REQUESTS AND REQUESTS THE
024022,002314:                                                                                                  #  ACTUAL RR DESIGNATION. INITIALLY A CHECK IS MADE TO SEE IF A
024023,002315:                                                                                                  #  REMODE (RADMODES BIT 14) IS REQUESTED OR IN PROGRESS. IF SO,
024024,002316:                                                                                                  #  CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO STDESIG AFTER ROUTINE REMODE IS
024025,002317:                                                                                                  #  EXECUTED. IF NO REMODE, STDESIG IS IMMEDIATELY CALLED WHERE
024026,002318:                                                                                                  #  FIRST THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS CHECKED. IF
024027,002319:                                                                                                  #  PRESENT, THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 10) IS REMOVED
024028,002320:                                                                                                  #  AFTER WHICH THE PROGRAM EXITS TO RDBADEND. IF THE REPOSITION
024029,002321:                                                                                                  #  FLAG IS NOT PRESENT, THE CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
024030,002322:                                                                                                  #  BIT 15) IS CHECKED. IF PRESENT, ON EXECUTIVE CALL IS IMMEDIATELY
024031,002323:                                                                                                  #  MADE FOR DODES AFTER WHICH A .5 SECOND WAIT IS INITIATED BEFORE
024032,002324:                                                                                                  #  REPEATING AT STDESIG. IF THE RR SEARCH ROUTINE (LRS24.1) IS DESIGNATING
024033,002325:                                                                                                  #  TO A NEW POINT (NEWPTFLG SET) THE CURRENT DESIGNATE TASK IS TERMINATED.
024034,002326:                                                                                                  #  IF CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE IS NOT WANTED, THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
024035,002327:                                                                                                  #  BIT 10) IS CHECKED. IF NOT PRESENT, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO ENDRADAR TO
024036,002328:                                                                                                  #  CHECK RR CDU FAIL BEFORE RETURNING TO THE CALLING PROGRAM. IF DESIGNATE
024037,002329:                                                                                                  #  IS STILL REQUIRED, DESCOUNT IS CHECKED TO SEE IF THE 30 SECONDS HAS
024038,002330:                                                                                                  #  EXPIRED BEFORE RECEIVING THE RR DATA GOOD (CHAN 33 BIT 4)
024039,002331:                                                                                                  #  SIGNAL. IF OUT OF TIME, PROGRAM ALARM 00503 IS REQUESTED, THE
024040,002332:                                                                                                  #  RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE AND RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE
024041,002333:                                                                                                  #  (CHAN 12 BITS 14,2) BITS REMOVED, AND THE DESIGNATE FLAG
024042,002334:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 10) REMOVED BEFORE EXITING TO RDBADEND. IF
024043,002335:                                                                                                  #  TIME HAS NOT EXPIRED, DESCOUNT IS DECREMENTED, THE
024044,002336:                                                                                                  #  EXECUTIVE CALL MADE FOR DODES, AND A .5 SECOND WAIT INITIATED
024045,002337:                                                                                                  #  BEFORE REPEATING THIS PROCEDURE AT STDESIG.
024046,002338: 
024047,002339:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
024048,002340:                                                                                                  #  WAITLIST CALL FROM STARTDES
024049,002341:                                                                                                  #  TCF BEGDES FROM DORREPOS
024050,002342:                                                                                                  #  TC STDESIG RETURNING, FROM REMODE
024051,002343: 
024052,002344:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
024053,002345:                                                                                                  #  DESCOUNT, RADMODES
024054,002346: 
024055,002347:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
024056,002348:                                                                                                  #  ENDRADAR, FINDVAC
024057,002349: 
024058,002350:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_  DODES
024059,002351: 
024060,002352:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  PROGRAM ALARM 00503 (30 SECONDS HAVE EXPIRED) WITH NO RR DATA
024061,002353:                                                                                                  #  GOOD (CHAN 33 BIT 4) RECEIVED WHEN LOCK-ON (STATE BIT 5) WAS REQUESTED.
024062,002354: 
024063,002355:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  TASKOVER (SEARCH PATTERN DESIGNATING TO NEW POINT)
024064,002356:                                                                                                  #  ENDRADAR (NO DESIGNATE - RADMODES BIT 10)
024065,002357:                                                                                                  #  RDBADEND (REPOSITION OR 30 SECONDS EXPIRED)
024066,002358: 
024067,002359: 25,2564           40110        BEGDES             CS       RADMODES

024113,002405:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  DODES
024114,002406: 
024115,002407:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
024116,002408:                                                                                                  #  DODES CALCULATES AND REQUESTS ISSUANCE OF RR GYRO TORQUE
024117,002409:                                                                                                  #  COMMANDS. INITIALLY THE CURRENT RR CDU ANGLES ARE STORED AND
024118,002410:                                                                                                  #  THE LOS HALF-UNIT VECTOR TRANSFORMED FROM STABLE MEMBER TO
024119,002411:                                                                                                  #  NAVIGATION BASE COORDINATES VIA SMNB IF NECESSARY. THE
024120,002412:                                                                                                  #  SHAFT AND TRUNNION COMMANDS ARE THEN CALCULATED AS FOLLOWS_
024121,002413:                                                                                                  #  + SHAFT = LOS  . (COS(S), 0, -SIN (S)) (DOT PRODUCT)
024122,002414:                                                                                                  #  -TRUNNION = LOS  . (SIN (T) SIN (S), COS (T), SIN (T) COS (S) )
024123,002415:                                                                                                  #  THE SIGN OF THE SHAFT COMMAND IS THEN REVERSED IF IN MODE 2
024124,002416:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 12) BECAUSE A RELAY IN THE RR REVERSES THE 
024125,002417:                                                                                                  #  POLARITY OF THE COMMAND. AT RRSCALUP EACH COMMAND IS
024126,002418:                                                                                                  #  SCALED AND IF EITHER, OR BOTH, OF THE COMMANDS IS GREATER THAN
024127,002419:                                                                                                  #  .5 DEGREES, MPAC +1 IS SET POSITIVE. IF A CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE 
024128,002420:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 15) IS DESIRED AND THE SEARCH ROUTINE IS NOT OPERATING,
024129,002421:                                                                                                  #  THE RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 14) IS CLEARED AND RROUT
024130,002422:                                                                                                  #  CALLED TO PUT OUT THE COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION (RADMODES BIT 11)
024131,002423:                                                                                                  #  IS IN PROGRESS. IF A CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE AND THE SEARCH ROUTINE IS
024132,002424:                                                                                                  #  OPERATING (SRCHOPT FLAG SET) THE TRACK ENABLE IS NOT CLEARED. IF NO
024133,002425:                                                                                                  #  CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE AND BOTH COMMANDS ARE NOT LESS THAN .5 DEGREES AS
024134,002426:                                                                                                  #  INDICATED BY MPAC +1, THE RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 14) IS
024135,002427:                                                                                                  #  CLEARED AND RROUT CALLED TO PUT OUT THE COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION
024136,002428:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 11) IS IN PROGRESS. IF BOTH COMMANDS ARE LESS THAN .5
024137,002429:                                                                                                  #  DEGREES AS INDICATED BY MPAC+1, THE RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE BIT
024138,002430:                                                                                                  #  (CHAN 12 BIT 14) IS CLEARED AND RROUT CALLED TO PUT OUT THE
024139,002431:                                                                                                  #  COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION (RADMODES BIT 11) IS IN
024140,002432:                                                                                                  #  PROGRESS. IF BOTH COMMANDS ARE LESS THAN .5 DEGREES, THE
024141,002433:                                                                                                  #  LOCK-ON FLAG (STATE BIT 5) IS CHECKED. IF NOT PRESENT, THE
024142,002434:                                                                                                  #  DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 10) IS CLEARED, THE RR ERROR
024143,002435:                                                                                                  #  COUNTER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2) IS CLEARED, AND ENDOFJOB
024144,002436:                                                                                                  #  CALLED. IF LOCK-ON IS DESIRED, THE RR AUTO TRACKER (CHAN 12
024145,002437:                                                                                                  #  BIT 14) IS ENABLED FOLLOWED BY A CHECK OF THE RECEIPT OF THE
024146,002438:                                                                                                  #  RR DATA GOOD (CHAN 33 BIT 4) SIGNAL. IF RR DATA GOOD
024147,002439:                                                                                                  #  PRESENT, THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 10) IS CLEARED,
024148,002440:                                                                                                  #  THE RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2) IS CLEARED,
024149,002441:                                                                                                  #  AND ENDOFJOB CALLED. IF RR DATA GOOD IS NOT PRESENT, RROUT
024150,002442:                                                                                                  #  IS CALLED TO PUT OUT THE COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION
024151,002443:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 11) IS IN PROGRESS AFTER WHICH THE JOB IS TERMINATED
024152,002444:                                                                                                  #  VIA ENDOFJOB.
024153,002445: 
024154,002446:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
024155,002447:                                                                                                  #  EXECUTIVE CALL EVERY .5 SECONDS FROM BEGDES.
024156,002448: 
024157,002449:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
024158,002450:                                                                                                  #  RRTARGET (HALF-UNIT LOS VECTOR IN EITHER SM OR NB COORDINATES),
024159,002451:                                                                                                  #  LOKONSW (STATE BIT 5), RRNBSW (STATE BIT 6), RADMODES
024160,002452: 
024161,002453:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
024162,002454:                                                                                                  #  READCDUS, SMNB, CDULOGIC, MAGSUB, RROUT
024163,002455:

Page 557 

024165,002457:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
024166,002458:                                                                                                  #  NONE
024167,002459: 
024168,002460:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
024169,002461: 
024170,002462:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  ENDOFJOB (ALWAYS)
024171,002463: 
024172,002464: 25,2626           00006        DODES              EXTEND                                         
024173,002465: 25,2627           30036                           DCA      CDUT

024445,002737:                                                                                                  #  RADAR RUPT READER (R20)
024446,002738: 
024447,002739:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE, WHICH IS INITIATED BY A RADAR RUPT, PROCESSES THE RADAR DATA AND UPDATES THE APPROPRIATE
024448,002740:                                                                                                  #  DSKY LIGHTS.

024450,002742: 25,2000                                           SETLOC   RADARUPT

024453,002745: 25,3157                                           COUNT*   $$/RRUPT

024458,002750: 25,3160           04007                           ROR      SUPERBNK                              #  SUPERBNK MUST BE SAVED BECAUSE RUPT
024459,002751: 25,3161           54016                           TS       BANKRUPT                              #  MAY EXIT VIA TASKOVER.
024460,002752: 25,3162           00006                           EXTEND

024462,002754:

024468,002760:

024471,002763:

024473,002765: 25,3173           51332                           INDEX    RADBITS

024475,002767:

025084,003376:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME: LRS22.1 (DATA READ SUBROUTINE 1)
025085,003377:                                                                                                  #  MOD. NO.: 1       BY:  P. VOLANTE  SDC           DATE:  11-15-66
025086,003378: 
025087,003379: 
025088,003380:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
025089,003381: 
025090,003382:                                                                                                  #  1) READS RENDEZVOUS RADAR RANGE AND RANGE-RATE,TRUNION AND SHAFT ANGLES,THREE CDU VALUES AND TIME. CONVERTS THIS
025091,003383:                                                                                                  #  DATA AND LEAVES IT FOR THE MEASUREMENT INCORPORATION ROUTINE (LSR22.3). CHECKS FOR THE RR DATA GOOD DISCRETE,FOR
025092,003384:                                                                                                  #  RR REPOSITION AND RR CDU FAIL
025093,003385: 
025094,003386:                                                                                                  #  2) COMPARES RADAR LOS WITH LOS COMPUTED FROM STATE VECTORS TO SEE IF THEY ARE WITHIN THREE DEGREES
025095,003387: 
025096,003388: 
025097,003389:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE: BANKCALL FOR LRS22.1
025098,003390: 
025099,003391: 
025100,003392:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED:
025101,003393: 
025102,003394:                                                                                                  #         RRRDOT   LPS20.1
025103,003395:                                                                                                  #         RRRANGE  BANKCALL
025104,003396:                                                                                                  #         RADSTALL CDULOGIC
025105,003397:                                                                                                  #         RRNB     SMNB
025106,003398:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT: RETURN TO CALLER+1 WITH MPAC SET TO +0
025107,003399: 
025108,003400: 
025109,003401:                                                                                                  #  ERROR EXITS: RETURN TO CALLER+1 WITH ERROR CODE STORED IN MPAC AS FOLLOWS:
025110,003402: 
025111,003403:                                                                                                  #               00001-ERROR EXIT 1-RR DATA NO GOOD (NO RR DATA GOOD DISCRETE OR RR CDU FAIL OR RR REPOSITION)
025112,003404:                                                                                                  #               00002-ERROR EXIT 2-RR LOS NOT WITHIN THREE DEGREES OF LOS COMPUTED FROM STATE VECTORS
025113,003405: 
025114,003406: 
025115,003407:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS:  521-COULD NOT READ RADAR DATA (RR DATA GOOD DISCRETE NOT PRESENT BEFORE AND AFTER READING THE RADAR)
025116,003408:                                                                                                  #   (THIS ALARM IS ISSUED BY THE RADAREAD SUBROUTINE WHICH IS ENTERED FROM A RADARUPT)
025117,003409: 
025118,003410: 
025119,003411:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT: RRLOSVEC- THE RR LINE-OF-SIGHT VECTOR(USED BY LRS22.2)-A HALF-UNIT VECTOR
025120,003412:                                                                                                  #          RM- THE RR RANGE READING(TO THE CSM) DP, IN METERS SCALED B-29(USED BY LRS22.2 AND LRS22.3)
025121,003413: 
025122,003414:                                                                                                  #     ALL OF THE FOLLOWING OUTPUTS ARE USED BY LRS22.3:
025123,003415: 
025124,003416:                                                                                                  #          RDOTM- THE RR RANGE-RATE READING,DP, IN METERS PER CENTISECOND, SCALED B-7
025125,003417:                                                                                                  #          RRTRUN-RR TRUNION ANGLE,DP,IN REVOLUTIONS,SCALED B0
025126,003418:                                                                                                  #          RRSHAFT-RR SHAFT ANGLE,DP,IN REVOLUTIONS,SCALED B0
025127,003419:                                                                                                  #          AIG,AMG,AOG-THE CDU ANGLES,THREE SP WORDS

025332,003624:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME - LSR22.3                                                  DATE - 29 MAY 1967
025333,003625:                                                                                                  #  MOD. NO 3                                                               LOG SECTION - P20-25
025334,003626:                                                                                                  #  MOD. BY - DANFORTH                                                      ASSEMBLY LEMP20S REV 10
025335,003627: 
025336,003628:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
025337,003629: 
025338,003630:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE COMPUTES THE B-VECTORS AND DELTA Q FOR EACH OF THE QUANTITIES MEASURED BY THE RENDEZVOUS
025339,003631:                                                                                                  #  RADAR.(RANGE,RANGE RATE,SHAFT AND TRUNNION ANGLES). THE ROUTINE CALLS THE INCORP1 AND INCORP2 ROUTINES
025340,003632:                                                                                                  #  WHICH COMPUTE THE DEVIATIONS AND CORRECT THE STATE VECTOR.
025341,003633: 
025342,003634:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE
025343,003635:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE IS PART OF P20 RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION FOR THE LM COMPUTER O NLY. THE ROUTINE IS ENTERED FROM
025344,003636:                                                                                                  #  R22LEM  ONLY AND RETURNS DIRECTLY TO R22LEM  FOLLOWING SUCCESSFUL INCORPORATION OF MEASURED DATA. IF THE
025345,003637:                                                                                                  #  COMPUTED STATE VECTOR DEVIATIONS EXCEED THE MAXIMUM PERMITTED. THE ROUTINE RETURNS TO R22LEM  TO DISPLAY
025346,003638:                                                                                                  #  THE DEVIATIONS. IF THE ASTRONAUT ACCEPTS THE DATA R22LEM  RETURNS TO    LSR22.3 TO INCORPORATE THE
025347,003639:                                                                                                  #  DEVIATIONS INTO THE STATE VECTOR. IF THE ASTRONAUT REJECTS THE DEVIATIONS, NO MORE MEASUREMENTS ARE
025348,003640:                                                                                                  #  PROCESSED FOR THIS MARK,I.E.,R22LEM  GETS THE NEXT MARK.
025349,003641: 
025350,003642: 
025351,003643:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
025352,003644:                                                                                                  #   WLINIT     LGCUPDTE     INTEGRV     INCORP1     ARCTAN
025353,003645:                                                                                                  #   GETULC     RARARANG     INCORP2     NBSM        INTSTALL
025354,003646: 
025355,003647:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
025356,003648:                                                                                                  #   CORRECTED LM OR CSM STATE VECTOR (PERMANENT)
025357,003649:                                                                                                  #   NUMBER OF MARKS INCORPORATED IN MARKCTR
025358,003650:                                                                                                  #   MAGNITUDE OF POSITION DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP METERS B-29
025359,003651:                                                                                                  #   MAGNITUDE OF VELOCITY DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP +2 M/CSEC B-7
025360,003652:                                                                                                  #   UPDATED W-MATRIX
025361,003653: 
025362,003654: 
025363,003655:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
025364,003656:                                                                                                  #   LM AND CSM STATE VECTORS
025365,003657:                                                                                                  #   W-MATRIX
025366,003658:                                                                                                  #   MARK TIME IN MKTIME
025367,003659:                                                                                                  #   RADAR RANGE IN RM METERS B-29
025368,003660:                                                                                                  #         RANGE RATE IN RDOTM METERS/CSES B-7
025369,003661:                                                                                                  #         SHAFT ANGLE IN RRSHAFT REVS.B0
025370,003662:                                                                                                  #         TRUNNION ANGLE IN RRTRUN REVS. B0
025371,003663:                                                                                                  #   GIMBAL ANGLES  INNER IN AIG
025372,003664:                                                                                                  #                  MIDDLE IN AMG
025373,003665:                                                                                                  #                  OUTER IN AOG
025374,003666:                                                                                                  #   REFSMMAT
025375,003667:                                                                                                  #   RENDWFLG
025376,003668:                                                                                                  #   NOANGFLG
025377,003669:                                                                                                  #   VEHUPFLG
025378,003670: 
025379,003671:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
025380,003672:                                                                                                  #   PUSHLIST--ALL
025381,003673:                                                                                                  #   MX, MY, MZ  (VECTORS)

025773,004065:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
025774,004066: 
025775,004067:                                                                                                  #  LSR22.4 IS THE ENTRY TO PERFORM LUNAR SURFACE NAVIGATION FOR THE LM
025776,004068:                                                                                                  #  COMPUTER ONLY. THIS ROUTINE COMPUTES THE B-VECTORS AND DELTA Q FOR RANGE
025777,004069:                                                                                                  #  AND RANGE RATE MEASURED BY THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR
025778,004070: 
025779,004071:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
025780,004072:                                                                                                  #   INSTALL   LGCUPDTE  INCORP1   RP-TO-R
025781,004073:                                                                                                  #   INTEGRV   GETULC    INCORP2
025782,004074: 
025783,004075:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
025784,004076:                                                                                                  #   CORRECTED CSM STATE VECTOR (PERMANENT)
025785,004077:                                                                                                  #   NUMBER OF MARKS INCORPORATED IN MARKCTR
025786,004078:                                                                                                  #   MAGNITUDE OF POSITION DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP METERS B-29
025787,004079:                                                                                                  #   MAGNITUDE OF VELOCITY DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP +2 M/CSEC B-7
025788,004080:                                                                                                  #   UPDATED W-MATRIX
025789,004081:

Page 596 

025791,004083:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
025792,004084:                                                                                                  #   LM AND CSM STATE VECTORS
025793,004085:                                                                                                  #   W-MATRIX
025794,004086:                                                                                                  #   MARK TIME IN MKTIME
025795,004087:                                                                                                  #   RADAR RANGE IN RM METERS B-29
025796,004088:                                                                                                  #         RANGE RATE IN RDOTM METERS/CSEC B-7
025797,004089:                                                                                                  #   VEHUPFLG
025798,004090: 
025799,004091:

025996,004288:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME LRS24.1   RR SEARCH ROUTINE
025997,004289:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO  0        BY  P VOLANTE  SDC          DATE 1-15-67
025998,004290: 
025999,004291: 
026000,004292:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
026001,004293: 
026002,004294:                                                                                                  #  DRIVES THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR IN A HEXAGONAL SEARCH PATTERN ABOUT THE LOS TO THE CSM (COMPUTED FROM THE CSM AND LM
026003,004295:                                                                                                  #  STATE VECTORS) CHECKING FOR THE DATA GOOD DISCRETE AND MONITORING THE ANGLE BETWEEN THE RADAR BORESIGHT AND THE
026004,004296:                                                                                                  #  LM +Z AXIS. IF THIS ANGLE EXCEEDS 30 DEGREES THE PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE ROUTINE IS CALLED TO PERFORM AN
026005,004297:                                                                                                  #  ATTITUDE MANEUVER.
026006,004298: 
026007,004299: 
026008,004300:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE - BANKCALL FOR LRS24.1
026009,004301: 
026010,004302: 
026011,004303:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
026012,004304: 
026013,004305:                                                                                                  #        LEMCONIC      R61LEM
026014,004306:                                                                                                  #        CSMCONIC      RRDESSM
026015,004307:                                                                                                  #        JOBDELAY      FLAGDOWN
026016,004308:                                                                                                  #        WAITLIST      FLAGUP
026017,004309:                                                                                                  #        RRNB          BANKCALL
026018,004310: 
026019,004311: 
026020,004312:                                                                                                  #  EXIT  - TO ENDOFJOB WHEN THE SEARCH FLAG (SRCHOPT) IS NOT SET
026021,004313: 
026022,004314: 
026023,004315:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
026024,004316: 
026025,004317:                                                                                                  #      DATAGOOD (SP)-FOR DISPLAY IN R1- 00000 INDICATES NO LOCKON
026026,004318:                                                                                                  #                                       11111 INDICATES LOCKON ACHIEVED
026027,004319:                                                                                                  #      OMEGAD   (SP)-FOR DISPLAY IN R2- ANGLE BETWEEN RR BORESIGHT VECTOR AND THE SPACECRAFT +Z AXIS
026028,004320: 
026029,004321:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
026030,004322:                                                                                                  #     SEARCH FLAG MUST BE SET
026031,004323:                                                                                                  #     LM AND CSM STATE VECTORS AND REFSMMAT MATRIX
026032,004324:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
026033,004325: 
026034,004326:                                                                                                  #     RLMSRCH      UXVECT
026035,004327:                                                                                                  #     VXRLM        UYVECT
026036,004328:                                                                                                  #     LOSDESRD     NSRCHPNT
026037,004329:                                                                                                  #     DATAGOOD     OMEGAD
026038,004330:                                                                                                  #     MPAC         PUSHLIST
026039,004331: 
026040,004332: 
026041,004333: 26,3444                                           COUNT*   $$/LRS24
